    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',

        state: 'apple_oauth_state_8a85e9bd-5db6-452f-b332-976613e8e8ee'

<span id="freeTextContainer6121366215745616880">A body was found in the living room of a concert pianist, shot to death. Yi-yun Lin, the deceased, was a foreign student from China.   <span id="freeText6121366215745616880" style="display:none">A body was found in the living room of a concert pianist, shot to death. Yi-yun Lin, the deceased, was a foreign student from China. No murder weapon was found on the scene, no sign of forced entry.<br /><br />It was seemingly a homicide, but who was the killer? All the evidence points to her boyfriend, the concert pianist, but Detective Paul Winderman of the Boston Police Department has his doubts. The victim's ex-husband has vowed revenge on several occasions. Someone from her past might also want her dead.<br /><br />The tale of the Mystery of Revenge is a melting pot of love, desire, jealousy and greed. Proceed with caution; the facts could be deceiving.</span>

I didn't expect it at all. <br/><br/>Definitely read The Mystery of Revenge! It's a quick and enjoyable read. I loved it!</span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer640100879" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14629992591292181329">This is a book more than just a mystery. The suspense keeps me going and I just can't wait to find out the ending of this mystery. Along the way of reading I can't help appreciating the well-woven plot as well as the beautiful and sentimental narration the writer reveals in her story telling. It is hard to find a clean book with this high level of entertainment. It is a good read!</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer2044313241592554002">This book was slow to start and I was a little disappointed with it. I'm used to my mystery novels having more action and suspense. This book was told in a past / present style by many of the characters, which made it a little hard to follow, plus I really don't remember the author stating the time period of the story. I was interested in how the Chinese immigrants came to America and how they made a life for themselves here. Yi-Yun and Fang Chen marry and start a life for themselves. Eventually</span>
  <span id="freeText2044313241592554002" style="display:none">This book was slow to start and I was a little disappointed with it. I'm used to my mystery novels having more action and suspense. This book was told in a past / present style by many of the characters, which made it a little hard to follow, plus I really don't remember the author stating the time period of the story. I was interested in how the Chinese immigrants came to America and how they made a life for themselves here. Yi-Yun and Fang Chen marry and start a life for themselves. Eventually, Yi-Yun gets bored with home life as Fang is working and studying all the time. This boredom leads her to another man, a struggling selfish concert pianist. The characters were hard to like, especially Yi-Yun, and most seemed one dimensional, selfish and shallow. I must say however, the ending was different and not what I expected. </span>
  <a data-text-id="2044313241592554002" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/666315250?book_show_action=true">Jul 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer666315250" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6683191342744737888">I received this book through the Goodreads Giveaway.<br/><br/>This book was a very quick read as it is only 160 pages long. It wasn't a bad story, I just felt like it was all over the place. It kept jumping back and forth in time and between characters. Which kind of disrupted the flow of the story, for me at least. The writer did a good job at keeping you wondering who the actual killer was. Usually I can figure out how its going to end half way through, but didn't really expect the ending I got.<br/><br/><br/></span>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('eiERDK5WyYZvx8qtPl/LJl1cJdILH5oPYUDtGb+4OkNthX3X7741iw/K2aYEFJUWlYM4RdoQiNiI5u1v4+PA9Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('QDmEq7bxS91p+sFWbsxLdiF+8uiVEBuxG+rAFi6qY45Xnehw9xm30An30l1UhxVG6aHvf0QfCWbyTMBgcvGZOA==')})
  }
//]]>
